# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
3sinx + 4cosx ^8bwM4uTv

If we can write our equations in the form Rsin(ax +- b) or Rcos(ax +- b), they can be used to model various oscillating things ^RoycqgGR

Put 3sinx + 4cosx in the form Rsin(x + a) ^3WexElfT

Put sinx + cosx in the form Rsin(x+a) ^fh0ktMPW

Put sinx - √(3)cosx in the form Rsin(x-a),  ^rjIXU6XZ

sinx + cosx = Rsinxcosa + Rcosxsina ^H0rYsTUu

Put 2cosθ + 5sinθ in the form Rcos(θ-a) where 0 < a < 90
Hence solve, for 0<θ<360, the equation 2cosθ + 5sinθ = 3 ^FBMfPRsj

Find the maximum value of 12cosθ + 5sinθ and give the smallest positive value of θ at which it arises ^tUAyEeY5
